Launching the claude -p subprocess\n    28→    - Waiting for completion (with timeout enforcement)\n    29→    - Returning a StepResult with appropriate status\n    30→\n    31→    The runner is NOT responsible for:\n    32→    - Retry logic (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    33→    - Gate checking (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    34→    - Step ordering (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    35→    \"\"\"\n    36→\n    37→    def __call__(\n    38→        self,\n    39→        step: Step,\n    40→        config: PipelineConfig,\n    41→        cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n    42→    ) -> StepResult: ...\n    43→\n    44→\n    45→def execute_pipeline(\n    46→    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    47→    config: PipelineConfig,\n    48→    run_step: StepRunner,\n    49→    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    50→    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n    51→    on_state_update: Callable[[dict], None] = lambda state: None,\n    52→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool] = lambda: False,\n    53→) -> list[StepResult]:\n    54→    \"\"\"Generic pipeline executor.\n    55→\n    56→    Processes steps in order. Each element in ``steps`` is either:\n    57→    - A single Step (executed sequentially)\n    58→    - A list[Step] (all steps in the list executed in parallel)\n    59→\n    60→    For each step:\n    61→    1. Call on_step_start(step)\n    62→    2. Call run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n    63→    3. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n    64→    4. If gate fails and attempts < retry_limit: retry (go to 2)\n    65→    5. If gate fails and attempts exhausted: HALT\n    66→    6. Call on_step_complete(step, result)\n    67→    7. Call on_state_update(updated_state_dict)\n    68→\n    69→    For parallel step groups:\n    70→    - All steps in the group run concurrently via _run_parallel_steps()\n    71→    - If any step in the group fails, remaining steps are cancelled\n    72→    - All results from the group must be PASS before proceeding\n    73→\n    74→    Returns list of all StepResults (one per step, flattened).\n    75→    \"\"\"\n    76→    all_results: list[StepResult] = []\n    77→\n    78→    for entry in steps:\n    79→        if cancel_check():\n    80→            break\n    81→\n    82→        if isinstance(entry, list):\n    83→            # Parallel step group\n    84→            for s in entry:\n    85→                on_step_start(s)\n    86→\n    87→            group_results = _run_parallel_steps(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check)\n    88→            all_results.extend(group_results)\n    89→\n    90→            for r in group_results:\n    91→                on_step_complete(r.step, r)\n    92→\n    93→            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n    94→\n    95→            # If any step in the group failed, halt\n    96→            if any(r.status != StepStatus.PASS for r in group_results):\n    97→                break\n    98→        else:\n    99→            # Sequential step\n   100→            result = _execute_single_step(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check, on_step_start, on_step_complete)\n   101→            all_results.append(result)\n   102→            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n   103→\n   104→            if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n   105→                break\n   106→\n   107→    return all_results\n   108→\n   109→\n   110→def _execute_single_step(\n   111→    step: Step,\n   112→    config: PipelineConfig,\n   113→    run_step: StepRunner,\n   114→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n   115→    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n   116→    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n   117→) -> StepResult:\n   118→    \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic and gate checking.\"\"\"\n   119→    on_step_start(step)\n   120→    max_attempts = step.retry_limit + 1  # retry_limit=1 means 2 attempts total\n   121→\n   122→    for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):\n   123→        if cancel_check():\n   124→            now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   125→            result = StepResult(\n   126→                step=step,\n   127→                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n   128→                attempt=attempt,\n   129→                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n   130→                started_at=now,\n   131→                finished_at=now,\n   132→            )\n   133→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   134→            return result\n   135→\n   136→        result = run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n   137→        result = StepResult(\n   138→            step=result.step,\n   139→            status=result.status,\n   140→            attempt=attempt,\n   141→            gate_failure_reason=result.gate_failure_reason,\n   142→            started_at=result.started_at,\n   143→            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n   144→        )\n   145→\n   146→        # If step has no gate, trust the StepRunner's status\n   147→        if step.gate is None:\n   148→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   149→            return result\n   150→\n   151→        # If runner already reported failure/timeout, skip gate check\n   152→        if result.status in (StepStatus.TIMEOUT, StepStatus.CANCELLED):\n   153→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   154→            return result\n   155→\n   156→        # Run gate check\n   157→        passed, reason = gate_passed(step.output_file, step.gate)\n   158→        if passed:\n   159→            result = StepResult(\n   160→                step=step,\n   161→                status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   162→                attempt=attempt,\n   163→                gate_failure_reason=None,\n   164→                started_at=result.started_at,\n   165→                finished_at=result.finished_at,\n   166→            )\n   167→            on_step_complete(step, result)\n   168→            return result\n   169→\n   170→        # Gate failed\n   171→        _log.info(\"Gate failed for step '%s' (attempt %d/%d): %s\", step.id, attempt, max_attempts, reason)\n   172→\n   173→        if attempt < max_attempts:\n   174→            continue  # report.tasks_not_attempted = len(report.remaining_task_ids)\n   271→    report.total_turns_consumed = sum(r.turns_consumed for r in task_results)\n   272→    report.total_duration_seconds = sum(\n   273→        r.duration_seconds for r in task_results\n   274→    )\n   275→\n   276→    return report\n   277→\n   278→\n   279→def check_budget_guard(ledger: TurnLedger | None) -> str | None:\n   280→    \"\"\"Pre-launch budget guard: returns a halt message if budget is insufficient.\n   281→\n   282→    Returns None if launch is allowed, or a descriptive message string\n   283→    if the budget is too low to launch a subprocess.\n   284→    \"\"\"\n   285→    if ledger is None:\n   286→        return None\n   287→    if ledger.can_launch():\n   288→        return None\n   289→ 295→def execute_phase_tasks(\n   296→    tasks: list[TaskEntry],\n   297→    config: SprintConfig,\n   298→    phase,\n   299→    ledger: TurnLedger | None = None,\n   300→    *,\n   301→    _subprocess_factory=None,\n   302→) -> tuple[list[TaskResult], list[str]]:\n   303→    \"\"\"Per-task subprocess orchestration loop.\n   304→\n   305→    Iterates over a task inventory, spawning one subprocess per task with\n   306→    budget allocation from the TurnLedger. Returns task results and a list\n   307→    of remaining (unattempted) task IDs if budget was exhausted.\n   308→\n   309→    Args:\n   310→        tasks: Ordered list of TaskEntry from the tasklist parser.\n   311→        config: Sprint configuration.\n   312→        phase: The Phase being executed.\n   313→        ledger: Optional TurnLedger for budget tracking.\n   314→        _subprocess_factory: Optional callable for testing; signature\n   315→            ``(task, config, phase) -> (exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes)``.\n   316→\n   317→    Returns:\n   318→        Tuple of (results, remaining_task_ids). remaining_task_ids is non-empty\n   319→        only when the loop halted due to budget exhaustion.\n   320→    \"\"\"\n   321→    results: list[TaskResult] = []\n   322→    remaining: list[str] = []\n   323→\n   324→    if not tasks:\n   325→        return results, remaining\n   326→\n   327→    for i, task in enumerate(tasks):\n   328→        started_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   329→\n   330→        # Budget check: can we launch?\n   331→        if ledger is not None and not ledger.can_launch():\n   332→            # Mark this and all subsequent tasks as skipped\n   333→            remaining = [t.task_id for t in tasks[i:]]\n   334→            for t in tasks[i:]:\n   335→                results.append(\n   336→                    TaskResult(\n   337→                        task=t,\n   338→                        status=TaskStatus.SKIPPED,\n   339→                        started_at=started_at,\n   340→                        finished_at=datetime.now(timezone.utc),\n   341→                    )\n   342→                )\n   343→            break\n   344→\n   345→        # Debit the minimum allocation upfront\n   346→        if ledger is not None:\n   347→            ledger.debit(ledger.minimum_allocation)\n   348→\n   349→        # Spawn subprocess for this task\n   350→        if _subprocess_factory is not None:\n   351→            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _subprocess_factory(\n   352→                task, config, phase\n   353→            )\n   354→        else:\n   355→            # Default: delegate to ClaudeProcess (real execution)\n   356→            exit_code, turns_consumed, output_bytes = _run_task_subprocess(\n   357→                task, config, phase\n   358→            )\n   359→\n   360→        finished_at = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n   361→\n   362→        # Determine task status from exit code\n   363→        if exit_code == 0:\n   364→            status = TaskStatus.PASS\n   365→        elif exit_code == 124:\n   366→            status = TaskStatus.INCOMPLETE\n   367→        else:\n   368→            status = TaskStatus.FAIL\n   369→\n   370→        # Reconcile budget: debit actual consumption, credit back pre-allocation\n   371→        if ledger is not None:\n   372→            # We pre-debited minimum_allocation; now adjust for actual turns\n   373→            actual = max(turns_consumed, 0)\n   374→            pre_allocated = ledger.minimum_allocation\n   375→            if actual > pre_allocated:\n   376→                ledger.debit(actual - pre_allocated)\n   377→            elif actual < pre_allocated:\n   378→                ledger.credit(pre_allocated - actual)\n   379→\n   380→        results.append(\n   381→            TaskResult(\n   382→                task=task,\n   383→                status=status,\n   384→                turns_consumed=turns_consumed,\n   385→                exit_code=exit_code,\n   386→                started_at=started_at,\n   387→                finished_at=finished_at,\n   388→                output_bytes=output_bytes,\n   389→            )\n   390→        )\n   391→\n   392→    return results, remaining\n   393→\n   394→\n   395→def _run_task_subprocess(\n   396→    task: TaskEntry,\n   397→    config: SprintConfig,\n   398→    phase,\n   399→) -> tuple[int, int, int]:\n   400→    \"\"\"Run a single task in a subprocess. Returns (exit_code, turns, output_bytes).\n   401→\n   402→    This is the real implementation that spawns a ClaudeProcess. For testing,\n   403→    callers of execute_phase_tasks pass _subprocess_factory instead.\n   404→    \"\"\"\n   405→    # Build a task-specific prompt\n   406→    prompt = (\n   407→        f\"Execute task {task.task_id}: {task.title}\\n\"\n   408→        f\"From phase file: {phase.file}\\n\"\n   409→        f\"Description: {task.description}\\n\"\n   410→    )\n   411→\n   412→    proc = ClaudeProcess.__new__(ClaudeProcess)\n   413→    proc.config = config\n   414→    proc.phase = phase\n   415→    from superclaude.cli.pipeline.process import ClaudeProcess as _Base\n   416→    _Base.__init__(\n   417→        proc,\n   418→        prompt=prompt,\n   419→        output_file=config.output_file(phase),\n   420→        error_file=config.error_file(phase),\n   421→        max_turns=config.max_turns,\n   422→        model=config.model,\n   423→        permission_flag=config.permission_flag,\n   424→        timeout_seconds=config.max_turns * 120 + 300,\n   425→        output_format=\"stream-json\",\n   426→    )\n   427→    proc.start()\n   428→    proc.wait()\n   429→    exit_code = proc._process.returncode if proc._process else -1\n   430→    output_path = config.output_file(phase)\n   431→    output_bytes = output_path.stat().st_size if output_path.exists() else 0\n   432→    # Turn counting is wired separately in T02.06\n   433→    return (exit_code if exit_code is not None else -1, 0, output_bytes)\n   434→\n   435→\n   436→def execute_sprint(config: SprintConfig):\n   437→    \"\"\"Main orchestration loop.\n   438→\n   439→    For each active phase:\n   440→    1. Launch claude -p subprocess\n   441→    2. Start output monitor thread\n   442→    3. Update TUI in a polling loop until process exits (with timeout)\n   443→    4. Decide whether to continue or halt\n   446→    \"\"\"\n   447→    # Pre-flight: verify claude binary is available before starting TUI/logging\n   448→    if shutil.which(\"claude\") is None:\n   449→        raise SystemExit(\n   450→            \"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH. \"\n   451→            \"Install Claude Code CLI before running sprint.\"\n   452→        )\n   453→\n   454→    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n   455→    signal_handler.install()\n   456→\n   457→    setup_debug_logger(config)\n   458→    import logging as _logging\n   459→    _dbg = _logging.getLogger(_DBG_NAME)\n   460→\n   461→    logger = SprintLogger(config)\n   462→    tui = SprintTUI(config)\n   463→    monitor = OutputMonitor(Path(\"/dev/null\"))  # Timeout (exit 124) -> TIMEOUT\n   720→    2. Non-zero exit -> ERROR\n   721→    3. Result file with EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT -> HALT\n   722→    4. When both CONTINUE and HALT appear\n   736→        # (conflicting signals), HALT wins — the stronger/safer outcome.\n   737→        upper = content.upper()\n   738→        has_continue = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in upper\n   739→        has_halt = \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in upper\n   740→        if has_halt:\n   741→            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n   742→        if has_continue:\n   743→            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n   744→        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PASS\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n   745→            return PhaseStatus.PASS\n   746→        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*FAIL(?:ED|URE)?\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n   747→            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n   748→        # PARTIAL result means tasks did not fully complete — treat as halt\n   749→        if re.search(r\"status:\\s*PARTIAL\\b\", content, re.IGNORECASE):\n   750→            return PhaseStatus.HALT\n   751→        return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n   752→\n   753→    if output_file.exists() and output_file.stat().st_size > 0:\n   754→        # Check for budget exhaustion: a subprocess that exits 0 but hit\n   755→        # error_max_turns produced no useful result — reclassify as INCOMPLETE\n   756→        # to trigger HALT instead of silent continuation.\n   757→        if detect_error_max_turns(output_file):\n   758→            return PhaseStatus.INCOMPLETE\n   759→        return PhaseStatus.PASS_NO_REPORT\n   760→\n   761→    return PhaseStatus.ERROR\n   762→"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":"toolu_01Lk4ygdRKa8ZZqkhmHw7sVR","session_id":"bd635163-6670-4590-bdad-9396d591e706","uuid":"87685760-fe43-4824-97ec-0571b466b285"}

Pipeline executor / execute_pipeline function\n\nYou asked for `src/superclaude/cli/sprint/executor.py`, but the actual generic `execute_pipeline` function is in:\n\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/executor.py`\n\n### Full signature\n```python\ndef execute_pipeline(\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    run_step: StepRunner,\n    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n    on_state_update: Callable[[dict], None] = lambda state: None,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool] = lambda: False,\n) -> list[StepResult]:\n```\n\n### High-level structure\n```python\ndef execute_pipeline(...):\n    all_results: list[StepResult] = []\n\n    for entry in steps:\n        if cancel_check():\n            break\n\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # parallel group\n            for s in entry:\n                on_step_start(s)\n\n            group_results = _run_parallel_steps(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check)\n            all_results.extend(group_results)\n\n            for r in group_results:\n                on_step_complete(r.step, r)\n\n            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n\n            if any(r.status != StepStatus.PASS for r in group_results):\n                break\n        else:\n            # sequential step\n            result = _execute_single_step(\n                entry, config, run_step, cancel_check, on_step_start, on_step_complete\n            )\n            all_results.append(result)\n            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n\n            if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n                break\n\n    return all_results\n```\n\n### Key single-step behavior\n```python\ndef _execute_single_step(...):\n    on_step_start(step)\n    max_attempts = step.retry_limit + 1\n\n    for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):\n        if cancel_check():\n            ...\n            return StepResult(status=StepStatus.CANCELLED, ...)\n\n        result = run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n        result = StepResult(... attempt=attempt ...)\n\n        if step.gate is None:\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        if result.status in (StepStatus.TIMEOUT, StepStatus.CANCELLED):\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        passed, reason = gate_passed(step.output_file, step.gate)\n        if passed:\n            result = StepResult(status=StepStatus.PASS, ...)\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        if attempt < max_attempts:\n            continue\n\n        result = StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=attempt,\n            gate_failure_reason=reason,\n            ...\n        )\n        on_step_complete(step, result)\n        return result\n```\n\n### Important Phase 5 implication\nCurrent executor logic does not branch on `step.gate_mode`. Pipeline executor / execute_pipeline function\n\nYou asked for `src/superclaude/cli/sprint/executor.py`, but the actual generic `execute_pipeline` function is in:\n\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/executor.py`\n\n### Full signature\n```python\ndef execute_pipeline(\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    run_step: StepRunner,\n    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n    on_state_update: Callable[[dict], None] = lambda state: None,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool] = lambda: False,\n) -> list[StepResult]:\n```\n\n### High-level structure\n```python\ndef execute_pipeline(...):\n    all_results: list[StepResult] = []\n\n    for entry in steps:\n        if cancel_check():\n            break\n\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # parallel group\n            for s in entry:\n                on_step_start(s)\n\n            group_results = _run_parallel_steps(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check)\n            all_results.extend(group_results)\n\n            for r in group_results:\n                on_step_complete(r.step, r)\n\n            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n\n            if any(r.status != StepStatus.PASS for r in group_results):\n                break\n        else:\n            # sequential step\n            result = _execute_single_step(\n                entry, config, run_step, cancel_check, on_step_start, on_step_complete\n            )\n            all_results.append(result)\n            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n\n            if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n                break\n\n    return all_results\n```\n\n### Key single-step behavior\n```python\ndef _execute_single_step(...):\n    on_step_start(step)\n    max_attempts = step.retry_limit + 1\n\n    for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):\n        if cancel_check():\n            ...\n            return StepResult(status=StepStatus.CANCELLED, ...)\n\n        result = run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n        result = StepResult(... attempt=attempt ...)\n\n        if step.gate is None:\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        if result.status in (StepStatus.TIMEOUT, StepStatus.CANCELLED):\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        passed, reason = gate_passed(step.output_file, step.gate)\n        if passed:\n            result = StepResult(status=StepStatus.PASS, ...)\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        if attempt < max_attempts:\n            continue\n\n        result = StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=attempt,\n            gate_failure_reason=reason,\n            ...\n        )\n        on_step_complete(step, result)\n        return result\n```\n\n### Important Phase 5 implication\nCurrent executor logic does not branch on `step.gate_mode`. GateResultQueue\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass TrailingGateResult:\n    \"\"\"Result of a trailing gate evaluation.\"\"\"\n\n    step_id: str\n    passed: bool\n    evaluation_ms: float\n    failure_reason: str | None = None\n\n\nclass GateResultQueue:\n    \"\"\"Thread-safe queue for collecting gate evaluation results.\n\n    Wraps stdlib ``queue.Queue`` with typed put/drain/pending_count methods.\n    Safe for concurrent access from multiple daemon threads.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        self._queue: Queue[TrailingGateResult] = Queue()\n        self._pending = 0\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    def put(self, result: TrailingGateResult) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Enqueue a gate result. Thread-safe.\"\"\"\n        self._queue.put(result)\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending += 1\n\n    def drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Collect all available results without blocking.\n\n        Returns a list of all results currently in the queue.\n        \"\"\"\n        results: list[TrailingGateResult] = []\n        while True:\n            try:\n                result = self._queue.get_nowait()\n                results.append(result)\n            except Empty:\n                break\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending = max(0, self._pending - len(results))\n        return results\n\n    def pending_count(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Return count of unprocessed results.\"\"\"\n        return self._queue.qsize()\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.01 -- TrailingGateRunner\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass TrailingGateRunner:\n    \"\"\"Daemon-thread gate evaluator for trailing gate mode.\n\n    Spawns daemon threads to evaluate gate criteria on step output files\n    after the step subprocess completes. Results are collected via the\n    internal GateResultQueue.\n\n    Thread safety: submit() and drain() may be called concurrently from\n    any thread. cancel() propagates to all active daemon threads.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, result_queue: GateResultQueue | None = None) -> None:\n        self._queue = result_queue or GateResultQueue()\n        self._threads: list[threading.Thread] = []\n        self._cancelled = threading.Event()\n        self._pending_count = 0\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    @property\n    def result_queue(self) -> GateResultQueue:\n        return self._queue\n\n    def submit(\n        self,\n        step: Step,\n        gate_check: Callable[[Path, GateCriteria], tuple[bool, str | None]] = gate_passed,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Spawn a daemon thread to evaluate gate criteria on step output.\n\n        The thread terminates after evaluation completes or cancellation.\n        \"\"\"\n        if step.gate is None:\n            # No gate to evaluate; submit a pass result immediately\n            self._queue.put(\n                TrailingGateResult(\n                    step_id=step.id,\n                    passed=True,\n                    evaluation_ms=0.0,\n                    failure_reason=None,\n                )\n            )\n            return\n\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending_count += 1\n\n        def _evaluate() -> None:\n            try:\n                if self._cancelled.is_set():\n                    return\n                start = time.monotonic()\n                passed, reason = gate_check(step.output_file, step.gate)\n                elapsed_ms = (time.monotonic() - start) * 1000\n                result = TrailingGateResult(\n                    step_id=step.id,\n                    passed=passed,\n                    evaluation_ms=elapsed_ms,\n                    failure_reason=reason,\n                )\n                self._queue.put(result)\n                _log.debug(\n                    \"Trailing gate for '%s': %s (%.1fms)\",\n                    step.id,\n                    \"PASS\" if passed else \"FAIL\",\n                    elapsed_ms,\n                )\n            except Exception:\n                _log.exception(\"Trailing gate evaluation error for step '%s'\", step.id)\n                self._queue.put(\n                    TrailingGateResult(\n                        step_id=step.id,\n                        passed=False,\n                        evaluation_ms=0.0,\n                        failure_reason=\"Gate evaluation raised an exception\",\n                    )\n                )\n            finally:\n                with self._lock:\n                    self._pending_count -= 1\n\n        t = threading.Thread(target=_evaluate, daemon=True)\n        self._threads.append(t)\n        t.start()\n\n    def drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Collect all completed gate results.\"\"\"\n        return self._queue.drain()\n\n    def wait_for_pending(self, timeout: float = 30.0) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Block until all pending gate evaluations complete or timeout.\n\n        Returns all accumulated results. Never hangs indefinitely.\n        \"\"\"\n        deadline = time.monotonic() + timeout\n        # Join all active threads with bounded timeout\n        for t in list(self._threads):\n            remaining = deadline - time.monotonic()\n            if remaining <= 0:\n                _log.warning(\"wait_for_pending timed out with %d threads still active\", self._pending_count)\n                break\n            t.join(timeout=remaining)\n\n        # Drain whatever results are available\n        return self.drain()\n\n    def cancel(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Signal cancellation to all pending daemon threads.\n\n        Threads check the cancellation event and terminate gracefully.\n        \"\"\"\n        self._cancelled.set()\n        # Give threads a brief window to notice cancellation\n        for t in list(self._threads):\n            t.join(timeout=1.0)\n        self._threads.clear()\n\n    @property\n    def pending_count(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Number of gate evaluations still in progress.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return self._pending_count\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.03 -- DeferredRemediationLog\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass RemediationStatus(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Status of a deferred remediation entry.\"\"\"\n\n    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    REMEDIATED = \"remediated\"\n    WAIVED = \"waived\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass RemediationEntry:\n    \"\"\"A single deferred remediation record.\"\"\"\n\n    step_id: str\n    gate_result: dict  # serialized TrailingGateResult\n    failure_reason: str\n    remediation_status: str = RemediationStatus.PENDING.value\n\n    def to_dict(self) -> dict:\n        return {\n            \"step_id\": self.step_id,\n            \"gate_result\": self.gate_result,\n            \"failure_reason\": self.failure_reason,\n            \"remediation_status\": self.remediation_status,\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, data: dict) -> RemediationEntry:\n        return cls(\n            step_id=data[\"step_id\"],\n            gate_result=data[\"gate_result\"],\n            failure_reason=data[\"failure_reason\"],\n            remediation_status=data.get(\"remediation_status\", RemediationStatus.PENDING.value),\n        )\n\n\nclass DeferredRemediationLog:\n    \"\"\"Persistent log of gate failures requiring remediation.\n\n    Single-writer thread safety: main thread writes, daemon threads may read.\n    Supports disk persistence for --resume recovery.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, persist_path: Path | None = None) -> None:\n        self._entries: list[RemediationEntry] = []\n        self._persist_path = persist_path\n        self._lock =       with self._lock:\n            self._entries.append(entry)\n        if self._persist_path:\n            self._write_to_disk()\n\n    def pending_remediations(self) -> list[RemediationEntry]:\n        \"\"\"Return all unresolved remediation entries.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return [\n                e for e in self._entries\n                if e.remediation_status == RemediationStatus.PENDING.value\n            ]\n\n    def mark_remediated(self, step_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Mark a remediation entry as resolved. Returns True if found.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            for entry in self._entries:\n                if entry.step_id == step_id and entry.remediation_status == RemediationStatus.PENDING.value:\n                    entry.remediation_status = RemediationStatus.REMEDIATED.value\n                    break\n            else:\n                return False\n        if self._persist_path:\n            self._write_to_disk()\n        return True\n\n    def serialize(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Serialize to JSON string for disk persistence.\"\"\"\n        with None) -> DeferredRemediationLog:\n        \"\"\"Recover state from JSON string for --resume support.\"\"\"\n        data = json.loads(json_str)\n        log = cls(persist_path=persist_path)\n        log._entries = [RemediationEntry.from_dict(d) for d in data]\n        return log\n\n    def _write_to_disk(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Persist current state to disk.\"\"\"\n        if self._persist_path is None:\n            return\n        self._persist_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n        self._persist_path.write_text(self.serialize(), encoding=\"utf-8\")\n\n    @classmethod\n    def load_from_disk(cls, path: Path) -> DeferredRemediationLog:\n        \"\"\"Load from disk if file exists, otherwise return empty log.\"\"\"\n        if path.exists():\n            content = path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n            return cls.deserialize(content, persist_path=path)\n        return cls(persist_path=path)\n\n    @property\n    def entry_count(self) -> int:\n        with self._lock:\n            return len(self._entries)\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.04 -- Scope-Based Gate Strategy\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass GateScope(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Scope levels for gate strategy resolution.\"\"\"\n\n    RELEASE = \"release\"\n    MILESTONE = \"milestone\"\n    TASK = \"task\"\n\n\ndef resolve_gate_mode(\n    scope: GateScope,\n    config_gate_mode: GateMode = GateMode.BLOCKING,\n    grace_period: int = 0,\n) -> GateMode:\n    \"\"\"Resolve the effective gate mode based on scope and configuration.\n\n    Rules:\n    - Release scope: ALWAYS BLOCKING (immutable, not configurable)\n    - Milestone scope: configurable, defaults to BLOCKING\n    - Task scope: TRAILING when grace_period > 0, else BLOCKING\n\n    Args:\n        scope: The gate scope level.\n        config_gate_mode: The configured gate mode (used for milestone scope).\n        grace_period: Grace period in seconds (used for task scope).\n\n    Returns:\n        The effective GateMode for this scope.\n    \"\"\"\n    if scope == GateScope.RELEASE:\n        # Release gates are ALWAYS blocking -- enforced invariant\n        return GateMode.BLOCKING\n\n    if scope == GateScope.MILESTONE:\n        # Milestone gates default to BLOCKING but are configurable\n Wraps stdlib ``queue.Queue`` with typed put/drain/pending_count methods.\n    Safe for concurrent access from multiple daemon threads.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        self._queue: Queue[TrailingGateResult] = Queue()\n        self._pending = 0\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n\n    def put(self, result: TrailingGateResult) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Enqueue a Thread-safe.\"\"\"\n        self._queue.put(result)\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending += 1\n\n    def drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]:\n        \"\"\"Collect all available results without blocking.\n\n        Returns a list of all results currently in the queue.\n        \"\"\"\n        results: list[TrailingGateResult] = []\n        while True:\n            try:\n                result = self._queue.get_nowait()\n                results.append(result)\n            except Empty:\n                break\n        with self._lock:\n            self._pending = max(0, self._pending - len(results))\n        return results\n\n    def pending_count(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Return count of unprocessed results.\"\"\"\n        return self._queue.qsize()\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# T05.01 -- TrailingGateRunner\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n\nclass TrailingGateRunner:\n    \"\"\"Daemon-thread gate evaluator for trailing gate mode.\n\n    Spawns daemon threads to evaluate gate criteria on step output files\n    after the step subprocess completes. \"\"\"Resolve the effective gate mode based on scope and configuration.\n\n    Rules:\n    - Release scope: ALWAYS BLOCKING (immutable, not configurable)\n    - Milestone scope: configurable, defaults The executor handles step ordering, retry logic,\nparallel dispatch, and state management.\n\nNFR-007: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport logging\nimport threading\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\nfrom typing import Callable, Protocol\n\nfrom .gates import gate_passed\nfrom .models import PipelineConfig, Step, StepResult, StepStatus\n\n_log = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.pipeline.executor\")\n\n\nclass StepRunner(Protocol):\n    \"\"\"Callable that executes a single step's subprocess and returns a result.\n\n    The runner is responsible for:\n    - Launching the claude -p subprocess\n    - Waiting for completion (with timeout enforcement)\n    - Returning a StepResult with appropriate status\n\n    The runner is NOT responsible for:\n    - Retry logic (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    - Gate checking (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    - Step ordering (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __call__(\n        self,\n        step: Step,\n        config: PipelineConfig,\n        cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n    ) -> StepResult: ...\n\n\ndef execute_pipeline(\n    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    run_step: StepRunner,\n    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n    on_state_update: Callable[[dict], None] = lambda state: None,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool] = lambda: False,\n) -> list[StepResult]:\n    \"\"\"Generic pipeline executor.\n\n    Processes steps in order. Each element in ``steps`` is either:\n    - A single Step (executed sequentially)\n    - A list[Step] (all steps in the list executed in parallel)\n\n    For each step:\n    1. Call on_step_start(step)\n    2. Call run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n    3. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n    4. If gate fails and attempts < retry_limit: retry (go to 2)\n    5. If gate fails and attempts exhausted: HALT\n    6. Call on_step_complete(step, result)\n    7. Call on_state_update(updated_state_dict)\n\n    For parallel step groups:\n    - All steps in the group run concurrently via _run_parallel_steps()\n    - If any step in the group fails, remaining steps are cancelled\n    - All results from the group must be PASS before proceeding\n\n    Returns list of all StepResults (one per step, flattened).\n    \"\"\"\n    all_results: list[StepResult] = []\n\n    for entry in steps:\n        if cancel_check():\n            break\n\n        if isinstance(entry, list):\n            # Parallel step group\n            for s in entry:\n                on_step_start(s)\n\n            group_results = _run_parallel_steps(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check)\n            all_results.extend(group_results)\n\n            for r in group_results:\n                on_step_complete(r.step, r)\n\n            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n\n            # If any step in the group failed, halt\n            if any(r.status != StepStatus.PASS for r in group_results):\n                break\n        else:\n            # Sequential step\n            result = _execute_single_step(entry, config, run_step, cancel_check, on_step_start, on_step_complete)\n            all_results.append(result)\n            on_state_update(_build_state(all_results))\n\n            if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n                break\n\n    return all_results\n\n\ndef _execute_single_step(\n    step: Step,\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    run_step: StepRunner,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a single step with retry logic and gate checking.\"\"\"\n    on_step_start(step)\n    max_attempts = step.retry_limit + 1  # retry_limit=1 means 2 attempts total\n\n    for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):\n        if cancel_check():\n            now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n            result = StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=attempt,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=now,\n                finished_at=now,\n            )\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        result = run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n        result = StepResult(\n            step=result.step,\n            status=result.status,\n            attempt=attempt,\n            gate_failure_reason=result.gate_failure_reason,\n            started_at=result.started_at,\n            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n        )\n\n        # If step has no gate, trust the StepRunner's status\n        if step.gate is None:\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # If runner already reported failure/timeout, skip gate check\n        if result.status in (StepStatus.TIMEOUT, StepStatus.CANCELLED):\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # Run gate check\n        passed, reason = gate_passed(step.output_file, step.gate)\n        if passed:\n            result = StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.PASS,\n                attempt=attempt,\n                gate_failure_reason=None,\n                started_at=result.started_at,\n                finished_at=result.finished_at,\n            )\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # Gate failed\n        _log.info(\"Gate failed for step '%s' (attempt %d/%d): %s\", step.id, attempt, max_attempts, reason)\n\n        if attempt < max_attempts:\n            continue  # retry\n\n        # Exhausted retries\n        result = StepResult(\n            step=step,\n            status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n            attempt=attempt,\n            gate_failure_reason=reason,\n            started_at=result.started_at,\n            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n        )\n        on_step_complete(step, result)\n        return result\n\n    # Should not reach here, but safety fallback\n    now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n    return StepResult(\n        step=step,\n        status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n        attempt=max_attempts,\n        gate_failure_reason=\"Unexpected: exhausted retry loop\",\n        started_at=now,\n        finished_at=now,\n    )\n\n\ndef _run_parallel_steps(\n    steps: list[Step],\n    config: PipelineConfig,\n    run_step: StepRunner,\n    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n) -> list[StepResult]:\n    \"\"\"Run steps concurrently. Returns when all complete or one fails.\n\n    Cross-cancellation: if any step fails after retry, a shared Event\n    is set, causing remaining steps to terminate their subprocesses.\n    \"\"\"\n    cancel_event = threading.Event()\n    results: list[StepResult | None] = [None] * len(steps)\n\n    def _worker(idx: int, step: Step) -> None:\n        def combined_cancel() -> bool:\n            return cancel_check() or cancel_event.is_set()\n\n        result = _execute_single_step(step, config, run_step, combined_cancel)\n        results[idx] = result\n        if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n            cancel_event.set()\n\n    threads = [\n        threading.Thread(target=_worker, args=(i, s), daemon=True)\n        for i, s in enumerate(steps)\n    ]\n    for t in threads:\n        t.start()\n    for t in threads:\n        t.join()\n\n    # Replace None entries (shouldn't happen, but defensive)\n    final: list[StepResult] = []\n    for i, r in enumerate(results):\n        if r is not None:\n            final.append(r)\n        else:\n            now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n            final.append(StepResult(\n                step=steps[i],\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=0,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Thread did not produce a result\",\n                started_at=now,\n                finished_at=now,\n            ))\n\n    return final\n\n\ndef _build_state(results: list[StepResult]) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Build a state dict from accumulated results.\"\"\"\n    return {\n        \"steps\": {\n            r.step.id: {\n                \"status\": r.status.value,\n                \"attempt\": r.attempt,\n                \"gate_failure_reason\": r.gate_failure_reason,\n            }\n            for r in results\n        },\n        \"total\": len(results),\n        \"passed\": sum(1 for r in results if r.status == StepStatus.PASS),\n        \"failed\": sum(1 for r in results if r.status.is_failure),\n    }\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":15,"oldLines":7,"newStart":15,"newLines":8,"lines":[" from typing import Callable, Protocol"," "," from .gates import gate_passed","-from .models import PipelineConfig, Step, StepResult, StepStatus","+from .models import GateMode, PipelineConfig, Step, StepResult, StepStatus","+from .trailing_gate import TrailingGateRunner"," "," _log = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.pipeline.executor\")"," "]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

Each element in ``steps`` is either:\n    - A single Step (executed sequentially)\n    - A list[Step] (all steps in the list executed in parallel)\n\n    For each step:\n    1. Call on_step_start(step)\n    2. Call run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n    3. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n       - BLOCKING mode: evaluate synchronously, halt on failure\n       - TRAILING mode (grace_period > 0): submit to TrailingGateRunner,\n         continue execution; sync point at end collects results\n    4. If gate fails and attempts < retry_limit: retry (go to 2)\n    5. If gate fails and attempts exhausted: HALT\n    6. Call on_step_complete(step, result)\n    7. Returns when all complete or one fails.\n\n    Cross-cancellation: if any step fails after retry, a shared Event\n    is set, causing remaining steps to terminate their subprocesses.\n    \"\"\"\n    cancel_event = threading.Event()\n    results: list[StepResult | None] = [None] * len(steps)\n\n    def _worker(idx: int, step: Step) -> None:\n        def combined_cancel() -> bool:\n            return cancel_check() or cancel_event.is_set()\n\n        result = _execute_single_step(step, config, run_step, combined_cancel)\n        results[idx] = result\n        if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n            cancel_event.set()\n\n    threads = [\n        threading.Thread(target=_worker, args=(i, s), daemon=True)\n        for i, s in enumerate(steps)\n    ]\n    for t in threads:\n        t.start()\n    for t in threads:\n        t.join()\n\n    # retry_limit=1 means 2 attempts total\n\n    # Determine effective gate mode\n    effective_mode = step.gate_mode\n    if config.grace_period == 0:\n        effective_mode = GateMode.BLOCKING\n\n    for attempt in range(1, max_attempts + 1):\n        if cancel_check():\n            now = datetime.now(timezone.utc)\n            result = StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n                attempt=attempt,\n                gate_failure_reason=\"Cancelled by external signal\",\n                started_at=now,\n                finished_at=now,\n            )\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        result = run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n        result = StepResult(\n            step=result.step,\n            status=result.status,\n            attempt=attempt,\n            gate_failure_reason=result.gate_failure_reason,\n            started_at=result.started_at,\n            finished_at=result.finished_at,\n        )\n\n        # If step has no gate, trust the StepRunner's status\n        if step.gate is None:\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # If runner already reported failure/timeout, skip gate check\n        if result.status in (StepStatus.TIMEOUT, StepStatus.CANCELLED):\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # TRAILING mode: submit to runner, return PASS immediately\n        if effective_mode == GateMode.TRAILING and trailing_runner is not None:\n            trailing_runner.submit(step)\n            result = StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.PASS,\n                attempt=attempt,\n                gate_failure_reason=None,\n                started_at=result.started_at,\n                finished_at=result.finished_at,\n            )\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # BLOCKING mode: run gate check synchronously\n        passed, reason = gate_passed(step.output_file, step.gate)\n        if passed:\n            result = StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=StepStatus.PASS,\n                attempt=attempt,\n                gate_failure_reason=None,\n                started_at=result.started_at,\n                finished_at=result.finished_at,\n            )\n            on_step_complete(step, result)\n            return result\n\n        # test_concurrent_submit_drain(self, tmp_path):\n        \"\"\"Concurrent submit/drain scenarios work correctly.\"\"\"\n        runner = TrailingGateRunner()\n        num_steps = 5\n\n        for i in range(num_steps):\n            step = _make_step(step_id=f\"step-{i}\", gate=None, tmp_path=tmp_path)\n            runner.submit(step)\n\n        # All should produce results\n        results = runner.wait_for_pending(timeout=5.0)\n        # Also drain any that arrived after wait\n        results.extend(runner.drain())\n        assert len(results) == num_steps\n        step_ids = {r.step_id for r in results}\n        assert step_ids == {f\"step-{i}\" for i in range(num_steps)}\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# T05.03 --             step_id=f\"w-{i}\", passed=False,\n                    evaluation_ms=float(i), failure_reason=f\"fail-{i}\",\n                ))\n\n        def reader():\n            for _ in range(20):\n       r1 = threading.Thread(target=reader)\n        r2 = threading.Thread(target=reader)\n        w.start()\n        r1.start()\n        r2.start()\n        w.join()\n        r1.join()\n        r2.join()\n\n        assert len(errors) == 0\n        assert log.entry_count == 20\n\n\n# ===========================================================================\n# T05.04 -- Scope-Based Gate
